            "title": "厦门鼓浪屿海鲜餐厅排行榜 · （上）", 
            "content": "<p>许多人提起鼓浪屿都会想到小清新、咖啡馆，又或者是日光岩……我和我的朋友们却不是为了这些而来。 </p><p>在鼓浪屿申遗成功的第一个旅游淡季我们来到鼓浪屿，寻找的不是情怀，而是<b>海鲜</b>。不少人觉得鼓浪屿商业现象太严重了，压根儿没什么靠谱的美食存在，曾经我也这么认为。</p><p>但鼓浪屿的这六家良心海鲜餐厅，让我明白在对于食物的态度上，每个人都有截然不同的认识，而对鼓浪屿的喜爱，只增不减。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-919fd707c026f61b66dd61356820fd8b_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"338\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-919fd707c026f61b66dd61356820fd8b_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-919fd707c026f61b66dd61356820fd8b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;600&#39; height=&#39;338&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"338\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-919fd707c026f61b66dd61356820fd8b_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-919fd707c026f61b66dd61356820fd8b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-919fd707c026f61b66dd61356820fd8b_b.gif\"/></figure><h2><b>TOP.6  一口本垟菜</b></h2><p>在鼓浪屿一座老洋房里，据说建于1930年，说是老洋房，其实入眼全是红砖墙，复古感扑面而来。翻着菜单斟酌片刻，选了几个菜，不一会就上菜了，速度可见一斑。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b9c1786f2591d29e2b61c04f2e96f615_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"464\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b9c1786f2591d29e2b61c04f2e96f615_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;700&#39; height=&#39;464&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"464\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b9c1786f2591d29e2b61c04f2e96f615_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b9c1786f2591d29e2b61c04f2e96f615_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>鱼酥卷</b></p><p>鱼酥卷是类似春卷的一种食物，外层是炸的焦脆的金黄色，包裹着鱼肉胡萝卜，再撒上肉松。</p><p>口感新奇而且清爽鲜美，不会有传统肉馅春卷的油腻，非常适合作开胃小菜。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e9340900a2cc7fb2e7c7603d9aacd37b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"464\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e9340900a2cc7fb2e7c7603d9aacd37b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;700&#39; height=&#39;464&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"464\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e9340900a2cc7fb2e7c7603d9aacd37b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e9340900a2cc7fb2e7c7603d9aacd37b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>干贝竹笙豆腐汤</b></p><p>这道颜色清爽的汤可不能小觑，碗底沉着干贝、豆腐，还有口感清脆的竹笙与竹荪，使得这汤十分鲜美。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-32e1dad8ba1c9b1ee59af6a2a6fb847e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"464\" data-rawheight=\"700\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"464\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-32e1dad8ba1c9b1ee59af6a2a6fb847e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;464&#39; height=&#39;700&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"464\" data-rawheight=\"700\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"464\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-32e1dad8ba1c9b1ee59af6a2a6fb847e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-32e1dad8ba1c9b1ee59af6a2a6fb847e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>海瓜子</b></p><p>炒海瓜子算是海边的一道特色菜吧，我总是很喜欢点这道菜。推荐这道，是因为这里的海瓜子比我以前吃的大个。</p><p>不知道是品种不同还是品质比较好，里面的肉更肥嫩饱满，烹制入味，一颗一颗慢慢品尝，是配酒好菜。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-38303f5c99afe7f4d7a1c085bcc163ec_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"784\" data-rawheight=\"520\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"784\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-38303f5c99afe7f4d7a1c085bcc163ec_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;784&#39; height=&#39;520&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"784\" data-rawheight=\"520\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"784\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-38303f5c99afe7f4d7a1c085bcc163ec_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-38303f5c99afe7f4d7a1c085bcc163ec_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>农家酸菜焖脆笋</b></p><p>酸菜焖脆笋的分量不多不少，酸菜不怎么酸，笋的味道很鲜，吃起来非常爽口，汤汁竟然也是鲜甜的，只可惜油略微有点多。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ef7fa1aeb6c28ac881f0f72fe5c844d8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"464\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ef7fa1aeb6c28ac881f0f72fe5c844d8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;700&#39; height=&#39;464&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"464\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ef7fa1aeb6c28ac881f0f72fe5c844d8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ef7fa1aeb6c28ac881f0f72fe5c844d8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>招牌海鲜焖面</b></p><p>也许这家店比较注重卖相，这道面也不例外，轻柔的橙黄色，点缀着鲜绿的配菜，海鲜面的汤汁里融入了海鲜的鲜美，面的口感比较松软，非常入味。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2603c99eee45e9509e1cf1c46dfe5842_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"573\" data-rawheight=\"430\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"573\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2603c99eee45e9509e1cf1c46dfe5842_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;573&#39; height=&#39;430&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"573\" data-rawheight=\"430\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"573\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2603c99eee45e9509e1cf1c46dfe5842_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2603c99eee45e9509e1cf1c46dfe5842_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>有一些菜单上的菜由于当天买不到就会没有，说明食材还是蛮新鲜的。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>地址：</b>鼓浪屿安海路59号</p><p><b>电话：</b>0592-2066066</p><p><b>时间：</b>11:00-21:30</p><p><b>推荐：</b>干贝竹笙豆腐汤 海鲜焖面 一口豆腐 一口杭椒芥味虾</p><p><b>慎点：</b>姜母鸭，嚼不动</p><p><b>人均：</b>102元</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>推荐理由：</b>上菜速度快</p><p><b>不足之处：</b>桌子间隔较小；服务有所欠缺；份量少</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>TOP.5  挑食 | 海鲜餐厅</b></h2><p>「挑食」位于一栋两层别墅的二楼，装修布置的很文艺，格调挺清新的，四周都没有遮挡，采光很好。</p><p>我最喜欢的位置是那个阳台，暖暖的阳光照在身上，很舒服。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-049d997ff7c0dd892bc35f865a0afb07_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"530\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-049d997ff7c0dd892bc35f865a0afb07_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;530&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"530\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-049d997ff7c0dd892bc35f865a0afb07_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-049d997ff7c0dd892bc35f865a0afb07_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>清蒸波士顿龙虾</b></p><p>落座点餐之后，大盘的龙虾端上桌，红红的壳白白的肉看着很是诱人，吃起来肉质饱满弹牙，紧实鲜美，大钳子里也满满都是肉，吃的都是满足。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-febf1298dac67e6ef4644ae3bb002988_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"530\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-febf1298dac67e6ef4644ae3bb002988_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;530&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"530\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-febf1298dac67e6ef4644ae3bb002988_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-febf1298dac67e6ef4644ae3bb002988_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>清蒸青斑鱼</b></p><p>青斑鱼的个头很大，以至于要分两个盘子才能装下，肉质厚实细嫩，鲜美可口，烹制的鲜香够味，无奈胃内存不足，实在是吃不完了。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c74b9fda33d83c5551566399d3014804_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"530\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c74b9fda33d83c5551566399d3014804_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;530&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"530\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c74b9fda33d83c5551566399d3014804_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c74b9fda33d83c5551566399d3014804_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>清蒸太子蟹</b></p><p>清蒸太子蟹，也叫珍宝蟹，个大多肉的蟹在盘子上十分诱人。迫不及待徒手拿起一块，果然是肉质饱满鲜甜，果然名不虚传。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a7f9a0ad80cc61c1179db9f60775c1cd_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"530\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a7f9a0ad80cc61c1179db9f60775c1cd_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;530&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"530\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a7f9a0ad80cc61c1179db9f60775c1cd_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a7f9a0ad80cc61c1179db9f60775c1cd_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>海蛎煎</b></p><p>这是闽南名菜之一，但是做的好吃的店家寥寥无几。在朋友们审视的目光下，我一口吃下。</p><p>海蛎十分饱满多汁，其中加了地瓜粉也很Q弹，配上浓郁的蛋香，蘸着厦门辣酱吃更是美味。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1afeef0695acb7729b4ca09ba87fa0f9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"530\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1afeef0695acb7729b4ca09ba87fa0f9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;530&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"530\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1afeef0695acb7729b4ca09ba87fa0f9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1afeef0695acb7729b4ca09ba87fa0f9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>地址：</b>鼓浪屿福建路15号(近海天堂构,毓园)</p><p><b>电话：</b>0592-2062398</p><p><b>时间：</b>10:00-21:30</p><p><b>推荐：</b>挑食豆腐 清蒸石斑鱼 深海野生蟹粥 清蒸波士顿龙虾</p><p><b>慎点：</b>船屋拌饭类似酱油水捞饭，加上很多海蛎，偏咸（¥58）</p><p><b>人均：</b>114元 </p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>推荐理由：</b>服务比较热情；菜的份量足</p><p><b>不足之处：</b>环境老旧，菜品种类较少</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>TOP.4  渔铺丨私厨</b></h2><p>「渔铺」隐藏在小巷子里，面积不大但环境优雅，与挑食的家常感不同，渔铺将深沉的黑色和古朴的原木自然的融合在一起，简单的布局让人很舒服。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-17e5ad4f3e15c3fcca80e1fb1b8b29f7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"666\" data-rawheight=\"413\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"666\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-17e5ad4f3e15c3fcca80e1fb1b8b29f7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;666&#39; height=&#39;413&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"666\" data-rawheight=\"413\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"666\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-17e5ad4f3e15c3fcca80e1fb1b8b29f7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-17e5ad4f3e15c3fcca80e1fb1b8b29f7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>醉煎蟹</b></p><p>寒冷的冬季，很多海鲜已经不好吃了，但冬蟹却还是很肥美。朋友们都对这道蟹赞不绝口。</p><p>蟹肉饱满鲜美，而且每一只都有膏。灌上高粱酒烹煮，酒香弥漫，中和了蟹的些许凉性，好吃又养生。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-49ec962c860747dec751a6dc305a2a1a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"408\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-49ec962c860747dec751a6dc305a2a1a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;408&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"408\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-49ec962c860747dec751a6dc305a2a1a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-49ec962c860747dec751a6dc305a2a1a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>茶树菇爆牡蛎</b></p><p>茶树菇用油走过，不酥脆，口感是茶树菇本身甜甜的，牡蛎作为佐料份量是不多，但很鲜，汁水迸发的时候加上茶树菇的香甜，中和的很棒，一点也不腻。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a612b7cdbbb2b01072120254cf77a30a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"525\" data-rawheight=\"552\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"525\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a612b7cdbbb2b01072120254cf77a30a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;525&#39; height=&#39;552&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"525\" data-rawheight=\"552\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"525\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a612b7cdbbb2b01072120254cf77a30a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a612b7cdbbb2b01072120254cf77a30a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>干煎本港带鱼</b></p><p>冬季的带鱼为了越冬做好了充足的准备，体内积蓄了脂肪，所以肉厚油润。</p><p>带鱼烹饪后的肉质鲜美香甜，经过小火煎制，很好的保持了带鱼本来的味道，表皮香脆，肉质鲜嫩。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9b349968216da2bf1588a3f727afbb42_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"407\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9b349968216da2bf1588a3f727afbb42_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;407&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"407\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9b349968216da2bf1588a3f727afbb42_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9b349968216da2bf1588a3f727afbb42_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>酱油水黄翅鱼</b></p><p>上菜的时候惊讶了一下，因为是两条黄翅鱼分成两个碗槽，看起来有点奇怪。</p><p>好在黄翅鱼的肉质比较细嫩且味道鲜美，加了酱油调味依然很清淡可口。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-64432fa7fa5b65a393870e87b31fb003_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"525\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-64432fa7fa5b65a393870e87b31fb003_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-09261e26241dbf1c39b15ecf435244a1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-09261e26241dbf1c39b15ecf435244a1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>地址：</b>开禾路111号（八市菜市场里）</p><p><b>时间：</b>7：00-19:00</p><p><b>推荐：</b>炸五香、米筛目</p><p><b>人均：</b>3元/人</p><h2><b>「惠源面包店HUI YUAN」</b></h2><p>要说到儿时记忆，</p><p>首当其冲还应该是五指面包和炸面包。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fcd1e289cabb0da133e7a3e9021a3d09_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fcd1e289cabb0da133e7a3e9021a3d09_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0b11363e8169a1a15c5003c11992c412_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0b11363e8169a1a15c5003c11992c412_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>炸面包里裹着火腿、小葱段、乡巴佬卤蛋等，</p><p>炸过的面包外表滚着椰丝，外皮酥脆，</p><p>面包外皮焦香内里微甜，内陷咸鲜香。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5df5b3450e1ecbc1457e520c2805b56f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"480\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5df5b3450e1ecbc1457e520c2805b56f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "content": "<p></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e64cfbdc9c9d84a953b8da11b685c67b_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e64cfbdc9c9d84a953b8da11b685c67b_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e64cfbdc9c9d84a953b8da11b685c67b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;427&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e64cfbdc9c9d84a953b8da11b685c67b_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e64cfbdc9c9d84a953b8da11b685c67b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e64cfbdc9c9d84a953b8da11b685c67b_b.gif\"/></figure><p>天上龙肉，地上驴肉。要说在中国吃驴肉的历史呢，那可得追溯至明朝1600年，至今已有500年之久。<br/></p><p>驴肉肉质细滑，高蛋白质脂肪低，不上火，吃到满意都不胖。</p><p>而且驴肉中的氨基酸丰富，它含有动物胶等营养成分，能很好地调养身体，在冬天吃驴肉进补是最好不过了。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-92983c86735d1756fe2a8a14043433a0_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"387\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-92983c86735d1756fe2a8a14043433a0_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-92983c86735d1756fe2a8a14043433a0_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;600&#39; height=&#39;387&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"387\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-92983c86735d1756fe2a8a14043433a0_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-92983c86735d1756fe2a8a14043433a0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-92983c86735d1756fe2a8a14043433a0_b.gif\"/></figure><p>冬天，又是各种刷火锅的节奏，花样繁多的火锅挑动着味蕾，涮完牛肉，吃羊肉，吃完羊肉刷海鲜，各种肉吃得味蕾鲜香。</p><p>But，在羊肉，牛肉，海鲜火锅遍地开花的厦门，你有没有试过驴肉火锅呢?</p><p>这阵子小编的朋友圈总被一张精致的小洋楼照片霸屏，一问才知道这是厦门首家驴肉火锅店--<b>潮驴</b>。</p><p>是的就是这栋两层的白色小洋房，吸引小编专门去吃了趟，</p><p>印象中火锅店都是古香古色的，这么洋气现代的火锅店倒是头一次见。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-04df5ece10bd16abfb51f719e478fb95_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-04df5ece10bd16abfb51f719e478fb95_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;427&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-04df5ece10bd16abfb51f719e478fb95_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-04df5ece10bd16abfb51f719e478fb95_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>踏入店中，马上就被店内悬挂的一片勺子所吸引，虽然不是特别理解这种风格，但是看上去还是蛮独特的，起码第一眼就能吸引人的眼球。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8b7c5d538c7f14851d43026ac474d256_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8b7c5d538c7f14851d43026ac474d256_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;427&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8b7c5d538c7f14851d43026ac474d256_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8b7c5d538c7f14851d43026ac474d256_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>整个店内呈简约大方的风格，在纯色基底上用灯光冷暖交错，总是讨喜。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bd4c67558f4ea7a5353de537663fa5c0_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"639\" data-rawheight=\"426\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"639\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bd4c67558f4ea7a5353de537663fa5c0_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;639&#39; height=&#39;426&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"639\" data-rawheight=\"426\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"639\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bd4c67558f4ea7a5353de537663fa5c0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bd4c67558f4ea7a5353de537663fa5c0_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>潮驴的驴肉都是每天现杀，新鲜供应的，在明档窗口看到师傅手起刀落的帅气身影~</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f422a151ead32537fa75a162f619b887_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"430\" data-rawheight=\"286\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f422a151ead32537fa75a162f619b887_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"430\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f422a151ead32537fa75a162f619b887_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;430&#39; height=&#39;286&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"430\" data-rawheight=\"286\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f422a151ead32537fa75a162f619b887_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"430\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f422a151ead32537fa75a162f619b887_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f422a151ead32537fa75a162f619b887_b.gif\"/></figure><p>我们点了一份驴骨汤底，份量十足，汤头浓郁。揭开锅盖，一股香浓中药味扑鼻而来。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ea0ea21deabcabee1d05b747b866c16c_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"225\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ea0ea21deabcabee1d05b747b866c16c_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"400\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;400&#39; height=&#39;225&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"225\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ea0ea21deabcabee1d05b747b866c16c_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"400\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ea0ea21deabcabee1d05b747b866c16c_b.gif\"/></figure><p>用勺捞起，原来独特地添加了草根以及各种四物，光是汤底就十分滋补养生。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ee429bd3cc223a03b651eafe56d36142_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"399\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ee429bd3cc223a03b651eafe56d36142_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;600&#39; height=&#39;399&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"399\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ee429bd3cc223a03b651eafe56d36142_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ee429bd3cc223a03b651eafe56d36142_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>驴肉性温，可补气养血，对女性有养颜，对男性则有壮阳之功效。而且驴肉鲜嫩，比牛羊肉更为高级。</p><p>驴肉也同样分为各种部位，驴舌、前胸肉、后腿肉、腱子肉等，每一种肉质与口感各不相同，相同的是令人惊艳的美味。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7cd0ef39f687cb79fdfc958734c085df_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"562\" data-rawheight=\"383\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"562\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7cd0ef39f687cb79fdfc958734c085df_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;562&#39; height=&#39;383&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"562\" data-rawheight=\"383\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"562\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7cd0ef39f687cb79fdfc958734c085df_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7cd0ef39f687cb79fdfc958734c085df_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>肩胛肉</b></p><p>驴的脂肪含量低，肩胛肉则是少数带有油脂的肉，所以入口特别滑嫩，一盘肉三两下就被抢光了~</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-93bb276628c14c04b6675a566f2704ec_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"909\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-93bb276628c14c04b6675a566f2704ec_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;909&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"909\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-93bb276628c14c04b6675a566f2704ec_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-93bb276628c14c04b6675a566f2704ec_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>值得一提的是 盘子旁边也都会备注该款驴肉应该涮的秒数，非常贴心。 </p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ab16ff560d1ed91ce217f8a29fc0b2e7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ab16ff560d1ed91ce217f8a29fc0b2e7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;427&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ab16ff560d1ed91ce217f8a29fc0b2e7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ab16ff560d1ed91ce217f8a29fc0b2e7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>里脊肉</b></p><p>里脊肉的口感则比较有嚼劲，如果你对肉类不了解，可以翻阅桌上的小册子查看驴肉分布图和相应介绍，也可以咨询wuli可爱的店员们。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7ba62d6b874700b3f5875299405b3f2b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7ba62d6b874700b3f5875299405b3f2b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;427&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7ba62d6b874700b3f5875299405b3f2b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7ba62d6b874700b3f5875299405b3f2b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>涮驴肉一般三上三下，肉质呈粉色就赶紧动筷子吧~</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0c1acd48b97859cd092e125a0559b453_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"293\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0c1acd48b97859cd092e125a0559b453_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"400\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;400&#39; height=&#39;293&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"293\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0c1acd48b97859cd092e125a0559b453_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"400\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0c1acd48b97859cd092e125a0559b453_b.gif\"/></figure><p><b>驴腩</b></p><p>驴腩，大块厚切，纹理清晰，肥瘦相间。扔入锅中稍烫片刻捞出，肉质鲜嫩无比，嚼劲十足。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7ff6df672dc65d8fa46df36c9e9616bb_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7ff6df672dc65d8fa46df36c9e9616bb_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;427&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a588e09d5ff4c0496cab0e10c13c9507_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a588e09d5ff4c0496cab0e10c13c9507_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>驴肉火烧</b>，烤的脆脆的面皮，里面塞满驴肉，一口下去，满满的幸福感！</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f3530106084ff010e17525bcde6cde46_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"420\" data-rawheight=\"328\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"420\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;443&#39; height=&#39;249&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"443\" data-rawheight=\"249\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-72ef40f278f0eb6b1e2651a6fc639919_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"443\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-72ef40f278f0eb6b1e2651a6fc639919_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-72ef40f278f0eb6b1e2651a6fc639919_b.gif\"/></figure><p>面线不仅为主食中的一种</p><p>也代表这闽南人情感和祝福的一种方式</p><p>闽南人祝寿贺喜要带面线，</p><p>亲友送行吃太平面线，</p><p>家中待客吃猪脚面线，如果办酒席或者孩子满月，</p><p>头道菜更是用面线，代表福寿绵长。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6632ae379153f6e028786eb2ea3f8e65_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"480\" data-rawheight=\"270\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6632ae379153f6e028786eb2ea3f8e65_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"480\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6632ae379153f6e028786eb2ea3f8e65_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;480&#39; height=&#39;270&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"480\" data-rawheight=\"270\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6632ae379153f6e028786eb2ea3f8e65_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"480\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6632ae379153f6e028786eb2ea3f8e65_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6632ae379153f6e028786eb2ea3f8e65_b.gif\"/></figure><p>看了小编的介绍， </p><p>大家是不是对这集非常感兴趣？ </p><p>其实，这已不是第一次</p><p>《舌尖》给厦门“打广告”了</p><p>节目前两季的总顾问沈宏非</p><p>也早就在他的微博中</p><p>表达过对厦门小吃的热爱了</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fc7c866f4a190794b7ed2f1749d6df36_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"584\" data-rawheight=\"503\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"584\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fc7c866f4a190794b7ed2f1749d6df36_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;690&#39; height=&#39;920&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"920\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a822c2af559a0a2bd48d5743f3f89aa1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a822c2af559a0a2bd48d5743f3f89aa1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>另外，你还觉得有哪些厦门美食，</b></p><p><b>有资格上《舌尖》？欢迎评论起来！</b></p>",

            "title": "厦门胡桃里 一个好吃又浪漫的音乐餐厅", 
            "content": "<p></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b2332bcf826e1d3b55199cc2d73a5bd2_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"227\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b2332bcf826e1d3b55199cc2d73a5bd2_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"400\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;400&#39; height=&#39;227&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"227\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b2332bcf826e1d3b55199cc2d73a5bd2_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"400\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b2332bcf826e1d3b55199cc2d73a5bd2_b.gif\"/></figure><p>“走到玉林路的尽头，坐在小酒馆的门口……”，赵雷的《成都》唱火了成都的小酒馆，而真正火遍中国的酒馆，是<b>「胡桃里」</b>。</p><p>最初我是不知道胡桃里音乐餐厅的，后来渐渐听说了它的名气，据说明星巡演的庆功会百分之八九十都在胡桃里举办的，这样的场面让我对它产生了非常大的好奇心。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7f06b37add2002d0740c84c8171e58fb_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"426\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7f06b37add2002d0740c84c8171e58fb_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;426&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"426\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7f06b37add2002d0740c84c8171e58fb_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7f06b37add2002d0740c84c8171e58fb_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>而我第一次去胡桃里，便是厦门这家东渡店。 </p><p>今天我早早地又来到这里，这次只有我自己。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-765ac51418a57eaa8fa64c46b2d58779_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"395\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-765ac51418a57eaa8fa64c46b2d58779_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;395&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"395\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-765ac51418a57eaa8fa64c46b2d58779_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-765ac51418a57eaa8fa64c46b2d58779_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>下午的胡桃里倒是和夜晚的昏暗不同，十分<b>自然清新</b>。靠着窗，外面就是大海，光线是非常充足的。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2b485e73bee5bd8e0688cc7aff5cb9c0_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"451\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2b485e73bee5bd8e0688cc7aff5cb9c0_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;451&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"451\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2b485e73bee5bd8e0688cc7aff5cb9c0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2b485e73bee5bd8e0688cc7aff5cb9c0_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>坐在巨大的鸟笼里，点上一杯咖啡，打开自己带来的书，看着看着入了神，丝毫感觉不到时间飞快地流逝。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-764526a967a91fc5e368a9d787be7ffb_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-764526a967a91fc5e368a9d787be7ffb_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;427&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"427\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-764526a967a91fc5e368a9d787be7ffb_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-764526a967a91fc5e368a9d787be7ffb_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>等我缓过神来，已经到了晚饭时间。等餐的时候，坐在落地窗前，耳边听着live享受着这份安静美好。</p><p>But，它并没有维持多久，烤鸡上桌的刹那立刻回神的吃货依旧是我。</p><h2><b>果木烤鸡</b></h2><p>说到胡桃里的美食，第一个要说的自然是招牌菜<b>果木烤鸡</b>，鸡皮烤得金黄香脆，油脂都被烘烤出去，只剩薄薄一层，咬一口，咸淡适中。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-cde8e501c5affcc3549aa69a4dd21cf0_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"302\" data-rawheight=\"220\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-cde8e501c5affcc3549aa69a4dd21cf0_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"302\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;302&#39; height=&#39;220&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"302\" data-rawheight=\"220\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-cde8e501c5affcc3549aa69a4dd21cf0_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"302\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-cde8e501c5affcc3549aa69a4dd21cf0_b.gif\"/></figure><p>肉质比较紧实，但不干柴，肉汁被牢牢锁住，滑嫩酥香，非常入味，配着能吃下一大碗饭，属于<b>强烈推荐</b>的一道菜。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b2332bcf826e1d3b55199cc2d73a5bd2_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"227\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b2332bcf826e1d3b55199cc2d73a5bd2_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"400\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;400&#39; height=&#39;227&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"227\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b2332bcf826e1d3b55199cc2d73a5bd2_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"400\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b2332bcf826e1d3b55199cc2d73a5bd2_b.gif\"/></figure><h2><b>沸腾水煮鱼</b></h2><p>热腾腾的水煮鱼一端上来，香味四溢，汤面被一层红彤彤的干辣椒覆盖，还未入口食欲已然沸腾。</p><p>夹起一片放入嘴里，唔~不会太辣，倒也鲜香滑嫩，总体来说比较普通。 </p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3c52dfd520cdf66ee4c5d232dff9d5f3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"426\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3c52dfd520cdf66ee4c5d232dff9d5f3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;426&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"426\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3c52dfd520cdf66ee4c5d232dff9d5f3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3c52dfd520cdf66ee4c5d232dff9d5f3_b.jpg\"/></figure><h2><b>西班牙墨鱼烤饭</b></h2><p>这道菜一开始只是因为好奇点的。上桌看着吸满了墨鱼汁的米饭，亲手挤上新鲜的柠檬汁。</p><p>入口不仅是满口的墨鱼香，更有柠檬的清新味道，以及鱿鱼、大虾、烧肉带来的多重口感。对于不喜墨鱼香的人不建议点这道。 </p><p>墨鱼汁富含丰富的营养价值，不仅可止血，制酸定痛，还能改善新陈代谢、增强免疫力，更具有抗癌效果，对缓和妇女更年期症状，抗衰老也有一定作用。但是这道菜的缺点就是会把牙齿弄得黑乎乎的。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7a4c15631ec990b62759c7b3ab2ce3cb_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"536\" data-rawheight=\"447\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"536\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7a4c15631ec990b62759c7b3ab2ce3cb_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;536&#39; height=&#39;447&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"536\" data-rawheight=\"447\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"536\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7a4c15631ec990b62759c7b3ab2ce3cb_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7a4c15631ec990b62759c7b3ab2ce3cb_b.jpg\"/></figure><h2><b>金枪鱼拌牛油果沙律</b></h2><p>金枪鱼外皮酥脆，内里却非常嫩滑，牛油果淡淡的奶香味更是为这道沙律增色了不少，口感层次分明，饭后来一口很爽口，就连平时不爱吃沙拉的我也停不住嘴。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-982a3fbe22f9c4385f21c4de52c09432_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"426\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-982a3fbe22f9c4385f21c4de52c09432_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;426&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"426\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-982a3fbe22f9c4385f21c4de52c09432_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-982a3fbe22f9c4385f21c4de52c09432_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>天色渐渐暗了下来，换上了微黄的小夜灯，直到八点胡桃里的“音乐会”开始了，夜也真正开始了。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1151f0a0e93b37dc77811f2aa8801c3c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"428\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1151f0a0e93b37dc77811f2aa8801c3c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;533&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7fa42269809778f4380f58c7f3a11846_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7fa42269809778f4380f58c7f3a11846_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>栗子馅</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a94614843a6477129141b3f367bfa6f4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a94614843a6477129141b3f367bfa6f4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "title": "厦门仁生果子的老板口气不小，说他家的果汁是最好喝的", 
            "content": "<p>仁生果子是什么？</p><p><b>仁生果子是一家有着40年历史的水果老店，主营不加水果汁、酱爆果捞、水果做的绵绵冰。</b></p><p>老板为了证明自家的产品是纯天然无添加，还会让你全程看着他如何制作。</p><p>店里很多饮品果盘都上过电视和报纸，为厦门小吃争了不少光。</p><p>想必这也是老板阿三敢自称他家的果汁是厦门最好喝的原因吧，毕竟产品足够好才敢这么嚣张。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-15d6bbcfd1798c9754021c20ca77c606_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"525\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-15d6bbcfd1798c9754021c20ca77c606_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;700&#39; height=&#39;525&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"525\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-15d6bbcfd1798c9754021c20ca77c606_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-15d6bbcfd1798c9754021c20ca77c606_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>进门左墙上的大菜单上最醒目的一句话：“厦门最好喝的果汁”，真是一家不懂得低调的饮品店啊。 </p><p>但它的老板却非常可爱，说自己的果汁是全厦门最好的，而且不接受任何反驳。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f626644f7dc82fedc2ea656f0467e17b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"525\" data-rawheight=\"700\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"525\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f626644f7dc82fedc2ea656f0467e17b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;525&#39; height=&#39;700&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"525\" data-rawheight=\"700\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"525\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f626644f7dc82fedc2ea656f0467e17b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f626644f7dc82fedc2ea656f0467e17b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>想必你们都很好奇这家店为何如此自信，看看他们家的产品你就知道了。</p><h2><b>酱 爆 果 捞</b></h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-69599bb2e476e2f7a7ca6ac11906bb01_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"525\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-69599bb2e476e2f7a7ca6ac11906bb01_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;700&#39; height=&#39;525&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"525\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-69599bb2e476e2f7a7ca6ac11906bb01_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-69599bb2e476e2f7a7ca6ac11906bb01_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>酱爆果捞就是选四种水果切丁凑满一盒，然后放到秘制的梅子汁里过一下再捞出来放回到盒子里。 </p><p>酱爆果捞的水果自己随便选，选满一杯为止，最后可以选择酸奶、百香果、巧克力等几种酱淋在水果上面。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-bb6d5a50d3b82debf4d9b4036401a59e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"525\" data-rawheight=\"594\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"525\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-bb6d5a50d3b82debf4d9b4036401a59e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;525&#39; height=&#39;594&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"525\" data-rawheight=\"594\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"525\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-bb6d5a50d3b82debf4d9b4036401a59e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-bb6d5a50d3b82debf4d9b4036401a59e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>水果在酸梅水里捞过，激发了水果本身的甜味，超级爽口好吃。 </p><p>可以选好多种水果，满满一杯吃起来很爽！</p><p>但可爱的老板竟说他不屑做这餐品，因为他家最好喝的是果汁！</p><p><b>建 议 </b>：爆浆果捞一定要加百香果酱，不要加芒果酱，芒果酱太甜了反而吃不到水果的本来甜味。</p><h2><b>鲜 榨 果 汁</b></h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1d0e48d67754c1d2bfbfef6476ffbf7d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"700\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1d0e48d67754c1d2bfbfef6476ffbf7d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;700&#39; height=&#39;700&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"700\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1d0e48d67754c1d2bfbfef6476ffbf7d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1d0e48d67754c1d2bfbfef6476ffbf7d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>为何老板敢说这是厦门最好喝的果汁？</p><p>最重要的原因是这家店的果汁不加水。</p><p>小伙伴们肯定会好奇，平时在家榨果汁都要加点水才行，不加水怎么榨汁？</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c6e8df881099d0c9fbeca6b48a6189d9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"394\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c6e8df881099d0c9fbeca6b48a6189d9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;700&#39; height=&#39;394&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"394\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c6e8df881099d0c9fbeca6b48a6189d9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c6e8df881099d0c9fbeca6b48a6189d9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>因为老板阿三是用现榨的甘蔗汁为辅，水果为主，在原汁机和榨汁机的工作下制作的果汁。</p><p>糖也不用加了，全靠甘蔗汁天然的甜味。</p><p>这样制作的果汁，比那些加水的果汁来的更健康，也更好喝。</p><p>难怪老板敢自称是厦门最好喝的果汁。</p><p>喝过以后，你不得不信，确实好喝！多了一些其他的味道，很特别。</p><p><b>建 议 </b>：可选金桔柠檬百香果汁、菠萝芒果汁、奇异果草莓汁、柠檬苹果汁等。</p><h2><b>水 果 绵 绵 冰 </b></h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-436c48dd933cfdf2244f7ebc2ab84178_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"465\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-436c48dd933cfdf2244f7ebc2ab84178_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;700&#39; height=&#39;465&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"465\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-436c48dd933cfdf2244f7ebc2ab84178_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-436c48dd933cfdf2244f7ebc2ab84178_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这家绵绵冰真的很好吃，没有加水，纯果汁制成，很细、入口即化。</p><p>用果汁和酸奶制作而成，牛油果香蕉这类水果会用甘蔗汁代替水，甜度刚刚好。</p><p>一份绵绵冰可以吃到两种水果的味道和甘蔗的清甜，可以说很值了，是夏天的最佳解暑良品。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7cbb9ad7591d55386bab8cc0be3f1677_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"394\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7cbb9ad7591d55386bab8cc0be3f1677_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;700&#39; height=&#39;394&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"394\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7cbb9ad7591d55386bab8cc0be3f1677_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7cbb9ad7591d55386bab8cc0be3f1677_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>绵绵冰的冰是果汁直接倒入制冰机制成的，好吃又健康，亲眼看老板制作，值得推荐。 </p><p>不止有芒果，还有榴莲、香蕉、猕猴桃等各种水果哦！       </p><h2><b>雪 冰 系 列</b></h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-5c7c48ab77290a49ed80f1cb5e17b4fd_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-5c7c48ab77290a49ed80f1cb5e17b4fd_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-5c7c48ab77290a49ed80f1cb5e17b4fd_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-5c7c48ab77290a49ed80f1cb5e17b4fd_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>老板新推出的鲜果榨汁雪冰系列！超级棒！</p><p>可以自己选底，配不一样的水果，比韩国雪冰好吃一万倍！ </p><p>都是真材实料，吃得出纯果味。  </p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-19588a1ce1f8294a7a2ac881566d7650_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"700\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-19588a1ce1f8294a7a2ac881566d7650_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;700&#39; height=&#39;700&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"700\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-19588a1ce1f8294a7a2ac881566d7650_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-19588a1ce1f8294a7a2ac881566d7650_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>小编也是先在网上看到他家的图片，才想去吃看看味道如何的。</p><p>看着这五颜六色的水果，口水都快要滴下来了！</p><p>先说说小编吃过的感觉吧：</p><p>水果是真的很新鲜，而且每样水果都非常好吃，不会涩、不会酸。</p><p>因为你选错水果的时候，老板会主动告诉你那样水果最好不要选，不好吃。</p><p>所以剩下的、你选中的水果，就是非常可口的啦！</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-17e84e1f41a11816011d9137da43952d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"515\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-17e84e1f41a11816011d9137da43952d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;700&#39; height=&#39;515&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"515\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-17e84e1f41a11816011d9137da43952d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-17e84e1f41a11816011d9137da43952d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>而且过滤的酸梅汁，调配的非常好，让水果都带了一点酸甜味，又不会破坏水果本身的味道，真的好评。 </p><p>这家店目前挑不出缺点，如果非要说，就是价格上有些偏贵吧，用买果汁和果捞的钱可以自己去买好多水果。</p><p>不过，谁让我们懒呢，喜欢吃现成的，既然要吃现成的，就要吃最好的！</p><p>最好的当然首选这家仁生果子啦。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>店名</b>：仁生果子</p><p><b>地址</b>：思明南路1号121(阿水烤鱼隔壁)</p><p><b>人均</b>：20元</p><p><b>电话</b>：15359297664 / 15959241746</p><p></p>",

            "content": "<p></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-81e909c914fa156959fc5ca91de89b02_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"427\" data-rawheight=\"240\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-81e909c914fa156959fc5ca91de89b02_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"427\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-81e909c914fa156959fc5ca91de89b02_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;427&#39; height=&#39;240&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"427\" data-rawheight=\"240\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-81e909c914fa156959fc5ca91de89b02_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"427\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-81e909c914fa156959fc5ca91de89b02_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-81e909c914fa156959fc5ca91de89b02_b.gif\"/></figure><p>7天的春节假期一眨眼就过去了，虽说假期是过去了，可假期里海吃海喝长的肉肉却非常碍眼的过不去，回来上班，同事见着的第一眼不是说新年好，而是，你！胖！了！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>看着自己整个冬天储存下来的脂肪，想想不久就要来的夏天，是不是很想把自己的肉肉甩掉呢。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>But，</b>你说白天上班没时间锻炼，晚上想去健身房，可那跑步机上永远都奔腾着人，想去夜跑，可又不知道哪里适合哪里安全....只能看着自己的小肚腩发愁！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>不要慌！今天小编就给你推荐几条风景好，道路宽还安全的夜跑路线，快点跑起来吧！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>初级版</b></p><p>〖<b> 海湾公园夜跑</b> 〗</p><p>海湾公园在厦门市湖滨西路西侧、厦门西海域和筼筜湖之间，公园用地总面积20.01万平方米，共有5大段，全长7.07公里。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-16386829f2e55cac6b729744877235f2_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"620\" data-rawheight=\"296\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"620\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-16386829f2e55cac6b729744877235f2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;620&#39; height=&#39;296&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"620\" data-rawheight=\"296\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"620\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-16386829f2e55cac6b729744877235f2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-16386829f2e55cac6b729744877235f2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>路面平坦宽阔，跑起来舒适，周边灯火通明，在这夜跑也很安全。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>园内可西眺大海，东望筼筜湖和白鹭洲公园，西北方向是海沧大桥，美丽的鼓浪屿也在视线之内。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-16754f53fe64cf343ee7c62e7ca6495f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"478\" data-rawheight=\"611\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"478\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-16754f53fe64cf343ee7c62e7ca6495f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;478&#39; height=&#39;611&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"478\" data-rawheight=\"611\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"478\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-16754f53fe64cf343ee7c62e7ca6495f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-16754f53fe64cf343ee7c62e7ca6495f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>浪漫的海，凉凉的风，清新的空气，在这里跑步一定会让人感到身心舒适。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3096f2749f1c0d465809a5ead890dc4a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"289\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3096f2749f1c0d465809a5ead890dc4a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;289&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"289\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3096f2749f1c0d465809a5ead890dc4a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3096f2749f1c0d465809a5ead890dc4a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>〖<b>湖边水库夜跑</b> 〗</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>湖边水库与在建的五缘湾片区和湖里高新技术园接壤，东侧与软件园二期和虎仔山相邻，</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>南侧为忠仑公园，西侧紧临金尚小区。成了周边居民夜晚出门的好去处。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ddb69bbe3f2d56ff4a6e305b497dbc3c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"496\" data-rawheight=\"265\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"496\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ddb69bbe3f2d56ff4a6e305b497dbc3c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;496&#39; height=&#39;265&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"496\" data-rawheight=\"265\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"496\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ddb69bbe3f2d56ff4a6e305b497dbc3c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ddb69bbe3f2d56ff4a6e305b497dbc3c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>整个的水库不大，但跑一圈也足够了，整个湖边都是树，道路也算宽敞。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>晚上很多小孩和老人在这里散步玩耍，既不会太热闹也不会太安静，塞着耳机，慢慢的跑，刚刚好。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-49ce55dfaf37038244c93233e8efa5b0_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"475\" data-rawheight=\"378\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"475\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-49ce55dfaf37038244c93233e8efa5b0_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;475&#39; height=&#39;378&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"475\" data-rawheight=\"378\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"475\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-49ce55dfaf37038244c93233e8efa5b0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-49ce55dfaf37038244c93233e8efa5b0_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>安全盲区：侯卿路金山湖景大厦旁，行人较少，周边树木茂盛。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>中级版</b></p><p>〖 <b>五缘湾夜跑 </b>〗</p><p>五缘湾跑一圈，总的路程差不多9km多，五缘湾的两侧每隔一段均有大桥相连接，沿湾的跑道近半多为木栈道跑道，基本没什么车辆，跑起来的也非常舒适。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-575064fb3737e8db9283e1e6db48f880_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"731\" data-rawheight=\"484\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"731\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-575064fb3737e8db9283e1e6db48f880_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;731&#39; height=&#39;484&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"731\" data-rawheight=\"484\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"731\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-575064fb3737e8db9283e1e6db48f880_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-575064fb3737e8db9283e1e6db48f880_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>同时有500多米长的纯净沙滩和100米左右长的河卵石健身沙滩，很适合大家休闲健身跑步。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0699740c1195d9a1a12a02e11a607864_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"399\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0699740c1195d9a1a12a02e11a607864_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;399&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"399\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0699740c1195d9a1a12a02e11a607864_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0699740c1195d9a1a12a02e11a607864_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>跑累了，散散步，看看海湾的夜景，也是非常惬意的事。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-67937fca54029bdfaf292c8c3dcfc00d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"364\" data-rawheight=\"364\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"364\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;300&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"300\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9a6d7510d9f2ad275bc1ee292ffe39ee_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9a6d7510d9f2ad275bc1ee292ffe39ee_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>而狐尾山也是看夜景的最佳位置，夜跑上去后俯瞰厦门夜景的感觉超棒！</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-087d5058a2b76b9f480e43fc656c9e28_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"732\" data-rawheight=\"335\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"732\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-087d5058a2b76b9f480e43fc656c9e28_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;408&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"408\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f7c4f21d0625500b67e104d1dbbbebe8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f7c4f21d0625500b67e104d1dbbbebe8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>一圈大约15公里，这里风景好，道路也好，重点是运动氛围也好！很适合运动。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c122c824be6b39f18fdf53c4645ec607_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"426\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c122c824be6b39f18fdf53c4645ec607_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;370&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"370\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b1fde609de1d33e6079db95b35da0742_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b1fde609de1d33e6079db95b35da0742_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>高级版</b></p><p>〖 <b>环岛路夜跑</b> 〗</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>作为厦门环海风景旅游干道之一的环岛路，不管是骑行，散步还是夜跑，都是再适合不过的地点了。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b7f7548d7695562798a2524073c4f4a5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"976\" data-rawheight=\"694\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"976\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b7f7548d7695562798a2524073c4f4a5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;976&#39; height=&#39;694&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"976\" data-rawheight=\"694\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"976\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b7f7548d7695562798a2524073c4f4a5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b7f7548d7695562798a2524073c4f4a5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>环岛路全程43公里，这样跑一圈下来，也足足有一个全程马拉松那么长了！ </p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>当然我们只要选择一段，就可以很舒适的完成今天的夜跑。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-11012def67a9418e8ca17349267b5ce1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1024\" data-rawheight=\"576\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1024\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-11012def67a9418e8ca17349267b5ce1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1024&#39; height=&#39;576&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1024\" data-rawheight=\"576\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1024\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-11012def67a9418e8ca17349267b5ce1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-11012def67a9418e8ca17349267b5ce1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>道路整洁平坦，宽广无比，风景尽收眼底。但晚上散步，骑行的人也是蛮多的，要注意避让哦。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-49673457551b6fd7b9bed98af1f02229_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"460\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-49673457551b6fd7b9bed98af1f02229_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;690&#39; height=&#39;460&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"460\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-49673457551b6fd7b9bed98af1f02229_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-49673457551b6fd7b9bed98af1f02229_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>晚上这里灯火通明，也有很多跑团在这里集体活动跑步，说不定可以遇到加入他们哟~</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f8eec386afb79eea0595387dbe17540b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"390\" data-rawheight=\"459\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"390\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;390&#39; height=&#39;459&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"390\" data-rawheight=\"459\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"390\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f8eec386afb79eea0595387dbe17540b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>安全盲区：台湾民俗村附近坡度较大。会展南路公交站往黄厝一带灯光较暗，行人较少，国际金融中心大厦到会展中心的沙滩旁甚至在节假日都没有什么行人</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>〖<b>筼筜湖公园夜跑</b>〗</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>筼筜湖一圈12公里，地处白鹭洲公园内，位于厦门岛西南部，在历史上这里曾经是一个天然的港湾，每当夜幕降临，停泊在港湾内的渔船灯光闪闪十分美丽。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-df7241aadd8625b0a5995a7f998edf1c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"412\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-df7241aadd8625b0a5995a7f998edf1c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;412&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"412\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-df7241aadd8625b0a5995a7f998edf1c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-df7241aadd8625b0a5995a7f998edf1c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这里的环湖绿道的建设也是十分不错，地面平坦，绿树成荫。不管是跑步环境，还是风景环境都是十分良好的。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d6ccbc476436b8e46f4c713be7dc6583_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"625\" data-rawheight=\"372\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"625\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d6ccbc476436b8e46f4c713be7dc6583_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;625&#39; height=&#39;372&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"625\" data-rawheight=\"372\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"625\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d6ccbc476436b8e46f4c713be7dc6583_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d6ccbc476436b8e46f4c713be7dc6583_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>夜景也是棒棒哒，晚上在这里跑跑步，感受感受独处的时光。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-582a64ad716100a5922757ecaf360408_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"960\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"960\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-582a64ad716100a5922757ecaf360408_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;960&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"960\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"960\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-582a64ad716100a5922757ecaf360408_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-582a64ad716100a5922757ecaf360408_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>身体和心灵同时跑在路上。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-47faa8caa759b53c6317b5b55e9a78d4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"558\" data-rawheight=\"395\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"558\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-47faa8caa759b53c6317b5b55e9a78d4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;558&#39; height=&#39;395&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"558\" data-rawheight=\"395\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"558\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-47faa8caa759b53c6317b5b55e9a78d4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-47faa8caa759b53c6317b5b55e9a78d4_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>安全盲区：筼筜雅游到湖滨中路一段，行人少，灯光暗；观鸟走廊靠湖滨西路一侧，木板遮挡，如有危险，外界不易察觉。此外，湖中桥下的木栈道没有灯，不少流浪汉在此歇息。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>好啦，厦门适合跑步的最佳地点有了，那还等啥，趁着好时光，赶紧换上装备，一起夜跑一起欣赏美丽的厦门吧！ </p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>TIPS</p><p><b>夜跑五个不要</b></p><p>1.不要佩戴首饰（避免遭到抢劫，以及方便跑步，不会被磕伤。）</p><p>2.不要把耳机开太大声（避免听不到喇叭声带来的危险。）</p><p>3.不要贪图凉快穿太少（尤其是现在的天气，晚上还是相对冷的，很容易生病！）</p><p>4.不要马上喝水（跑完步马上喝水会增加汗水的排出，使盐分损失更多，还会增加血液循环的量，从而加重心脏的负担。）</p><p>5.不要马上坐下（跑完步血液流通很快，心脏跳动急促，突然坐下的时候，下半身的血液流动减慢，不利于身体的自我调节，会造成心脏的负担。）</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c5bc1fcf4f609e9ef7255031e4fe2623_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"360\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c5bc1fcf4f609e9ef7255031e4fe2623_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c5bc1fcf4f609e9ef7255031e4fe2623_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;
