            "title": "最适合情侣去的厦门5个景点，单身狗慎点哦", 
            "content": "<p>厦门是一个浪漫且文艺的城市，所以不论你是两情相悦羞羞涩涩，还是浓情蜜意情到深处，亦或是牵手相伴平淡相交。</p><p>在厦门，总能找到适合你们表达爱意的地方。</p><p>在这个城市，无论是清晨亦或是黄昏，到处都弥漫着浪漫的气息。</p><p>如果你和你的那个Ta，不知道该牵手去哪里，就让小编给你们介绍几个适合约会的地方吧。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>鼓浪屿</b></h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3cfb4bae7cab76168b989629fe99b935_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"201\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3cfb4bae7cab76168b989629fe99b935_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"400\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;400&#39; height=&#39;201&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"201\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3cfb4bae7cab76168b989629fe99b935_b.jpg\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"400\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3cfb4bae7cab76168b989629fe99b935_b.gif\"/></figure><p>在厦门怎么少得了鼓浪屿。</p><p>这里是厦门最火爆的景点之一，入选了中国第52处世界遗产项目。</p><p>近几年游客增多，岛上变得拥挤，所以不知道该不该推荐给大家。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-edb6e2db2232984adb8cca53443b583a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"593\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-edb6e2db2232984adb8cca53443b583a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;593&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"593\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-edb6e2db2232984adb8cca53443b583a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-edb6e2db2232984adb8cca53443b583a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>但撇去游客多这个因素，鼓浪屿是真的非常适合情侣一起去玩的景点。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-06b7303411ed319538cb1e14836e48a1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"593\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-06b7303411ed319538cb1e14836e48a1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;593&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"593\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-06b7303411ed319538cb1e14836e48a1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-06b7303411ed319538cb1e14836e48a1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这里，随处都散发着文艺、清新的气息，随便某个角度，都能拍出美美的照片。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ad6c74c0fdc79e04778e9acef5aff1a8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ad6c74c0fdc79e04778e9acef5aff1a8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;533&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ad6c74c0fdc79e04778e9acef5aff1a8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ad6c74c0fdc79e04778e9acef5aff1a8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>在鼓浪屿，你可以和Ta一起逛有情怀、故事的小店，看看里面的手工艺品，购买属于你们的情侣纪念品。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-712cb0920afcecd1d54f8ed0b93461f6_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-712cb0920afcecd1d54f8ed0b93461f6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;533&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-712cb0920afcecd1d54f8ed0b93461f6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-712cb0920afcecd1d54f8ed0b93461f6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>和Ta一起吃遍岛上的美味，一起吃得圆滚滚，葛优躺在沙发上，看着彼此的模样甜蜜的笑。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-db09a8640c841e87d72220c974c22c0d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"810\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-db09a8640c841e87d72220c974c22c0d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;810&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"810\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-db09a8640c841e87d72220c974c22c0d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-db09a8640c841e87d72220c974c22c0d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>和Ta赏遍岛上民国时期留下的花园。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c76904338f4018332dac4e1f2881d13e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"610\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c76904338f4018332dac4e1f2881d13e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;610&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"610\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c76904338f4018332dac4e1f2881d13e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c76904338f4018332dac4e1f2881d13e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这里，有最浪漫的日出与日落。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-084683cc9faf288258f22195993379af_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"534\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-084683cc9faf288258f22195993379af_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;534&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"534\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-084683cc9faf288258f22195993379af_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-084683cc9faf288258f22195993379af_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>无论哪种场景，都非常适合两人一起分享。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b8b7083615abdef52fb3b2b0b988d7cb_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b8b7083615abdef52fb3b2b0b988d7cb_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;600&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b8b7083615abdef52fb3b2b0b988d7cb_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b8b7083615abdef52fb3b2b0b988d7cb_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>和Ta牵手走遍鼓浪屿所有浪漫的地方，留下满满的回忆。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>环岛路 木栈道</b></h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b127edac3c4b08012a9622aca14de471_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b127edac3c4b08012a9622aca14de471_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;690&#39; height=&#39;450&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b127edac3c4b08012a9622aca14de471_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b127edac3c4b08012a9622aca14de471_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>环岛路是厦门最美的一道风景线，可以在这骑单车、散步。</p><p>聆听海浪，轻拂海风，真的是一种享受。</p><p>这样浪漫的海边，最适合和心上人分享。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-16ab235829067308b1318f7327076d85_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-16ab235829067308b1318f7327076d85_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;690&#39; height=&#39;450&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-16ab235829067308b1318f7327076d85_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-16ab235829067308b1318f7327076d85_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>海滩上会有一些人在拍照、戏水，当你们看完海以后，想找个安静的地方散散步，就可以去木栈道了。</p><p>木栈道就在海滩边上，全长6公里。</p><p>或许刚从海滩走上木栈道时，还是觉得不够安静，但往里再走一些，就能享受两个人的风景了。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1b78b914924e9b466152218fa57f3909_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1b78b914924e9b466152218fa57f3909_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;690&#39; height=&#39;450&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1b78b914924e9b466152218fa57f3909_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1b78b914924e9b466152218fa57f3909_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>和恋人手牵手在木栈道漫步，海风徐徐。</p><p>此时此刻，不管你想说什么，有多肉麻，在温柔又广阔的海浪声的掩饰下，都不会觉得脸红了。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-51bb20c7748283dcf75ccc7c38036689_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-51bb20c7748283dcf75ccc7c38036689_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;690&#39; height=&#39;450&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-51bb20c7748283dcf75ccc7c38036689_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-51bb20c7748283dcf75ccc7c38036689_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>漫步在木栈道，时常会看到有新人在这里拍婚纱照。</p><p>此刻的你一定也希望，能和身边的Ta，走到最后吧。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>厦门大学 青春气息</b></h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0777de029b32a8bc806cdb8c628d44f2_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0777de029b32a8bc806cdb8c628d44f2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;690&#39; height=&#39;450&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0777de029b32a8bc806cdb8c628d44f2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0777de029b32a8bc806cdb8c628d44f2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>带Ta走进这青青校园，回忆过去校园里的青春气息。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-961f8e66fa569c7a738db75f2eb93290_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-961f8e66fa569c7a738db75f2eb93290_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;690&#39; height=&#39;450&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-961f8e66fa569c7a738db75f2eb93290_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-961f8e66fa569c7a738db75f2eb93290_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>两个人再走一遍校园的操场，再回味一遍初识的心动。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a03dab299ec5f73d0f0a57df12ddc7a3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"558\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a03dab299ec5f73d0f0a57df12ddc7a3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;558&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"558\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a03dab299ec5f73d0f0a57df12ddc7a3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a03dab299ec5f73d0f0a57df12ddc7a3_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>坐在芙蓉湖边的草坪上，谈上学的时光，谈心中的梦想，谈未来的方向。 </p><p>那种小欢喜的心情，是不是在心里跳跃？</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6ae50765077462e651cb613381512693_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6ae50765077462e651cb613381512693_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;690&#39; height=&#39;450&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6ae50765077462e651cb613381512693_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6ae50765077462e651cb613381512693_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>带Ta去看看厦大的建筑，多留下一些关于彼此的画面。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b2998e0ff2ce391c1ef37de281a61eb5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b2998e0ff2ce391c1ef37de281a61eb5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;690&#39; height=&#39;450&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b2998e0ff2ce391c1ef37de281a61eb5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b2998e0ff2ce391c1ef37de281a61eb5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>走走芙蓉隧道，欣赏别人留下的喷绘。</p><p>若恰好你也会绘画，就在墙上留下你们爱的告白吧。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0ef4941eb3484fb82aa752d33a6418bd_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0ef4941eb3484fb82aa752d33a6418bd_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;533&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0ef4941eb3484fb82aa752d33a6418bd_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0ef4941eb3484fb82aa752d33a6418bd_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>牵手去白城沙滩，静坐在沙滩上，迎着海风，眺望远方，看船只婆娑前行，享受那份悠闲恬静。</p><p>走向大海，海浪带着细沙，轻抚脚面，那种柔软和惬意会从脚底慢慢升起，舒缓身心。</p><p>在白城的沙滩上，一起用沙子堆出梦想中的城堡，是对你们未来最美好的期望。 </p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>方特梦幻王国</b></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bb736e266030e29a4b21435ee09eff64_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"458\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bb736e266030e29a4b21435ee09eff64_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;690&#39; height=&#39;458&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"458\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bb736e266030e29a4b21435ee09eff64_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bb736e266030e29a4b21435ee09eff64_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>位于同安的方特梦幻王国，就像一个少年时代所期待的游乐园。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ce75ae99b28d80bcf3d152ca19a7437a_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"275\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ce75ae99b28d80bcf3d152ca19a7437a_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ce75ae99b28d80bcf3d152ca19a7437a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;275&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"275\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ce75ae99b28d80bcf3d152ca19a7437a_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ce75ae99b28d80bcf3d152ca19a7437a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ce75ae99b28d80bcf3d152ca19a7437a_b.gif\"/></figure><p>这里有摩天轮浪漫的传说，有浪漫的爱情故事，惊险的恐龙岛。</p><p>恰似年幼时你我所期待的那样。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f57d5e8e6a597730765fc2648503dd14_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f57d5e8e6a597730765fc2648503dd14_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;533&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f57d5e8e6a597730765fc2648503dd14_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f57d5e8e6a597730765fc2648503dd14_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>在游玩中增加亲密，还原最初的那份童真。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-72f0d3aabdccd1e8253d62147ec65cf7_b.gif\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"338\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-72f0d3aabdccd1e8253d62147ec65cf7_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-72f0d3aabdccd1e8253d62147ec65cf7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;600&#39; height=&#39;338&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"338\" data-thumbnail=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-72f0d3aabdccd1e8253d62147ec65cf7_b.jpg\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-72f0d3aabdccd1e8253d62147ec65cf7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-72f0d3aabdccd1e8253d62147ec65cf7_b.gif\"/></figure><p>一起坐上旋转木马，体验电视剧里的浪漫情节。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f23057eac26ca6bcd66bcd9e87bfca_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f23057eac26ca6bcd66bcd9e87bfca_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;533&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f23057eac26ca6bcd66bcd9e87bfca_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f23057eac26ca6bcd66bcd9e87bfca_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>一起体验这些惊险刺激的项目，增进彼此之间的感情，让你不知不觉就爱上了这里。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>铁路公园 旧铁轨</b></h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-10dd796433e07c487dc539789ca4e4dd_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-10dd796433e07c487dc539789ca4e4dd_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-10dd796433e07c487dc539789ca4e4dd_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-10dd796433e07c487dc539789ca4e4dd_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这里原本是条废弃的老铁路，最近几年才被重新改造，从厦门站后面开始一直到和平码头附近。全长4.5公里。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4149d2aee124684a1e494538c873e5a8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"715\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4149d2aee124684a1e494538c873e5a8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;715&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"715\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4149d2aee124684a1e494538c873e5a8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4149d2aee124684a1e494538c873e5a8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>公园内有很独特的时光站台，一共有四个站点，分别是童年站，青年站，中年站，老年站。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-67f69d2cc1883be541437dcc8d8f3b6d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"662\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-67f69d2cc1883be541437dcc8d8f3b6d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1000&#39; height=&#39;662&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"662\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-67f69d2cc1883be541437dcc8d8f3b6d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-67f69d2cc1883be541437dcc8d8f3b6d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>每个站台旁的石凳，分别对应着靠背凳，转椅，沙发，摇椅，象征着人生四个阶段的轨迹。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1875587bba23a97d01c1b2b0783336c3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"715\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1875587bba23a97d01c1b2b0783336c3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;715&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"715\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1875587bba23a97d01c1b2b0783336c3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1875587bba23a97d01c1b2b0783336c3_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>带你的Ta到这里，一起牵手走过这四个站台，像不像与Ta经历了整个人生的不同阶段。 </p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-72f2d66e0c399ac3f398040fe02405e2_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"572\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-72f2d66e0c399ac3f398040fe02405e2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;572&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"572\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-72f2d66e0c399ac3f398040fe02405e2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-72f2d66e0c399ac3f398040fe02405e2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>与Ta走走这旧旧的铁轨，感受不一样的公园风景，让每个角落都有你们的回忆。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0cdffea08f2e138277bb7142679c8a2c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"359\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0cdffea08f2e138277bb7142679c8a2c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;600&#39; height=&#39;359&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"359\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0cdffea08f2e138277bb7142679c8a2c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0cdffea08f2e138277bb7142679c8a2c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>到了三角梅的花期，这里的花就会开得非常茂盛，充满了恋爱的粉红。</p><p>三角梅的花语是：“没有真爱是一种悲伤”。</p><p>与你身边的Ta在这里合照一张，“留下”你们此刻的真爱。</p><p></p><p></p>",
